    <script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
        var blocks = document.querySelectorAll('.my-reveal-code');
        blocks.forEach(function (block) {
            var seconds = parseInt(block.getAttribute('data-seconds')) || 15;
            var timeSpan = block.querySelector('.time');
            var codeSpan = block.querySelector('.the-code');
            var countdownSpan = block.querySelector('.countdown');
            if (!timeSpan || !codeSpan || !countdownSpan) return;

            timeSpan.textContent = seconds;

            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                seconds--;
                if (seconds <= 0) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    countdownSpan.style.display = 'none';
                    codeSpan.style.display = 'inline';
                } else {
                    timeSpan.textContent = seconds;
                }
            }, 1000);
        });
    });
    </script>
